style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">微信宣布<span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong>拍一拍可以撤回了！</strong></span>消息一出，直接上了微博热搜：</span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">   </span><img class=\" aligncenter\" style=\"width: 645px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important;\" title=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/10-1597587584.png\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？-20200817早读课\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" width=\"909\" height=\"auto\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">不少用户都在评论区表示，终于不用再担心，不小心在群里“拍了拍 leader 的屁股”了……</span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">      </span><img class=\" aligncenter\" style=\"width: 645px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important;\" title=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/4-1597587585.png\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？-20200817早读课\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" width=\"827\" height=\"auto\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">不过，这次微信改版的内容可不止有拍一拍，还有<span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong>微信的“新儿子”视频号，而且改动还非常大。</strong></span></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">改版后的视频号，不仅有了更大的转发界面、更多的引流入口，甚至还有了“私密功能”。</span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">接下来，我们就一起来看一看，视频号这波到底改了啥，以及改版会带来哪些影响吧。</span></p>\n<h2 style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px; font-size: 18px;\">01</span></strong></span></h2>\n<h2 style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px; font-size: 18px;\">这次视频号改了啥？</span></strong></span></h2>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">这次视频号的改动，说是“大刀阔斧”也不为过，转发界面便明显、有了可以不断下拉的兴趣推荐，还可以设置私密账号……</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">1）转发到朋友圈</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">改版之前，视频号分享到朋友圈是这样的：</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em; text-align: center;\"><img class=\" aligncenter\" style=\"background-color: #eeedeb; border: 1px solid #eeedeb; background-size: 22px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; height: 125.02267002518893px !important; width: 298px !important; background-position: center center; background-repeat: no-repeat no-repeat;\" title=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/7-1597587585.png\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？-20200817早读课\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" width=\"397\" height=\"auto\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">看上去很像一篇文章，用户只能看到视频号名字 &#38; 视频的标题，点开才能看到视频。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">这次改版后，转发到朋友圈的界面变成了“能看到视频封面，看不到文字标题”，点开视频就能看。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">同时，还新增了一个视频号账号入口，<span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong>点击视频下方的视频号名字，就可以直接进入账号主页</strong>，</span>查看 TA 的所有视频：</span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">     </span><img class=\" aligncenter\" style=\"width: 645px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important;\" title=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/10-1597587585.png\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？-20200817早读课\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" width=\"1545\" height=\"auto\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">2）转发到聊天界面</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">改版后，视频号内容转发到聊天界面变成了这样，也可以直接点击视频打开：</span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">     </span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">和转发到朋友圈不同的是，群里的视频没有作者主页入口，只能看视频。</span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">3）兴趣推荐</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">除了转发界面变更以外，视频号这次还有一个大动作：兴趣推荐。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">在朋友圈、聊天界面打开视频后，视频底部会有一个兴趣推荐，就像这样：</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em; text-align: center;\"><img class=\" aligncenter\" style=\"background-color: #eeedeb; border: 1px solid #eeedeb; background-size: 22px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; height: 164.74300254452928px !important; width: 285px !important; background-position: center center; background-repeat: no-repeat no-repeat;\" title=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/3-1597587587.png\" 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">再往下刷，就是微信算法给你推荐的视频，基本是<span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong>和你打开的视频同类型的内容。</strong></span></span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">4）评论可以切换账号</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">这次改版还多了一个新功能：评论时，可以自己选择视频号 / 微信号发送，就像这样：</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em; text-align: height=\"209px\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">如果使用视频号评论，那么在评论区的账号名字就是蓝色的；<strong>点击账号名，还可以直接进入该账号主页：</strong></span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">      </span><img class=\" aligncenter\" style=\"width: 645px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important;\" title=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/5-1597587588.png\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？-20200817早读课\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" width=\"1393\" height=\"auto\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">5）私密账号</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">在隐私设置里，可以开启「私密账号」。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">开启后<span style=\"color: #ff6600;\">，<strong>非关注者是看不到你的内容的。</strong></span>如果别人想关注你，必须发送申请，你同意以后才能关注，并看到内容。</span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">      </span><img class=\" aligncenter\" style=\"background-color: #eeedeb; border: 1px solid #eeedeb; background-size: 22px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; height: 429.6134316134316px !important; width: 645px !important; background-position: center center; background-repeat: no-repeat no-repeat;\" title=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/1-1597587588.png\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？-20200817早读课\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" width=\"1221\" height=\"auto\" /></p>\n<h2 style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px; font-size: 18px;\">02</span></strong></span></h2>\n<h2 style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px; font-size: 18px;\">这波改版带来什么影响</span></strong></span></h2>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">在今年 6 月，张小龙发了一条朋友圈：</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span></span></p>\n<blockquote>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #888888;\">2 亿，是个开始，mark 一下，因为再不 mark 就三亿四亿了。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #888888;\">数字容易，努力不易，需要很多很多思考，很多时间，很多人，很多次第二代，还有很多很多行代码……</span></p>\n</blockquote>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em; text-align: center;\"><img class=\" aligncenter\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; width: 261px !important; visibility: visible !important;\" title=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/10-1597587589.png\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？-20200817早读课\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">从中我们可以看到微信对于视频号的重视和信心，那么这波更新又会带来哪些影响呢？</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">1）微信为啥要这么做？</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">答案很简单，就是争夺用户，提高用户使用时长。</span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">具体到视频的这波改版，不论是对转发到朋友圈、聊天界面的优化、评论切换账号还是兴趣推荐，最核心的效果都是一个——引流。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">就拿视频号分享到朋友圈来说，改版后的<span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong>朋友圈引流效果是量级的提升。</strong></span></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">之前的展示与公众号文章类似，展示的主体是标题，用户打开时有明显的页面跳转。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em; text-align: center;\"><img class=\" aligncenter\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; width: 263px !important; visibility: visible !important;\" title=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/7-1597587590.png\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？-20200817早读课\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" width=\"263px\" height=\"256px\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">但改版后，直接展示的是封面大图，对<span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong>吸睛效果的提升</strong></span>是显而易见的。</span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">同时还省去了页面跳转，在朋友圈打开视频的使用体验非常流畅。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">对于个人来说可能只是多点一下的小问题，但<span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong>放在上亿用户规模下，跳转流失率是一个很大的优化。</strong></span></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em; text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">（动图）       <br style=\"max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" /></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">正如张小龙之前说的：</span></p>\n<blockquote>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #888888;\">一个人不管有多少好友，基本每个人每天在朋友圈里花的时长基本固定是 30 分钟左右。所以当朋友圈的半小时刷完之后，用户就会去找别的消遣，短视频是其中最多的选择。</span></p>\n</blockquote>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">现在微信正在逐步通过视频号和朋友圈的藕合，来消化用户在朋友圈之外，花在短视频上时间。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">虽然现在视频号的整体质量还并不算高，但随着视频号 DAU（日活）的快速提升，越来越多的主流短视频创作者都会多开一个视频号，<span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong>走“视频号+抖音+快手”多平台分发的模式。</strong></span></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">那当视频号和抖音快手的内容达到一定重合度时，视频号的截流效果会是非常可观的。</span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">     </span><img class=\" aligncenter\" style=\"font-size: 11pt; width: 645px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important;\" title=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/2-1597587591.png\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？-20200817早读课\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" width=\"1288\" height=\"auto\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">除了在深挖微信生态流量外，微信也在借鉴抖音快手的成功经验，来丰富视频号的运营手段。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">比如，评论可切换成视频号账号。</span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">通过在热门视频下占据热评，来吸引其他用户点进自己主页涨粉，是在抖音、快手等平台都验证过可行的低成本引流手段，在视频号也不例外。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em; text-align: center;\"><img class=\" aligncenter\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; width: 213px !important; visibility: visible !important;\" title=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/10-1597587593.png\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？-20200817早读课\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" width=\"213px\" height=\"419px\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">同样的，兴趣推荐对于引流的提升也很好理解。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">从这些更新里我们能很清楚的看到，微信正在一步一步地丰富视频号生态，和抖音快手争夺用户时长。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">2）未来怎么做视频号？</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">那么这次改版后，我们具体该如何做视频号呢？</span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">① 做好私域流量的精细化运营</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">这次改版之后，视频号的流量逻辑也越来越清楚了：私域撬动公域属性更加明显。</span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">我们都知道，抖音是一个纯“内容为王”的分发逻辑，不论你账号粉丝多少、之前播放多少，内容够好（受欢迎）就会爆，质量下降就会凉。</span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">但视频号则不然，私域流量的比重会非常高。就像你打开视频号的起始页，出现的是朋友点赞而不是热门视频推荐。</span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">尤其是在朋友圈直接以视频方式展示视频号后，私域流量的重要性还在提高。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em; text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages aligncenter\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; width: 105px !important; visibility: visible !important;\" title=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/7-1597587593.png\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？-20200817早读课\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">这里会有两个直接的利好，<span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong>第一个是冷启动更容易了</strong></span>，因为图像在朋友圈的引流效果会比文字好很多。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">第二个是精细化运营更加方便。</span></strong></span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">比如按照视频号的分发逻辑，我们在给视频预热时，最简单直接的方式就是找好友列表内对这类视频感兴趣的人点赞。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">借助这些私域流量，将视频辐射到他们的“朋友点赞”推荐页，从而撬动更大的公域流量</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">② 封面图比标题更重要</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">当然在这次改版后，具体的运营手段也和之前不大一样。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">比如之前的视频，想要在朋友圈获得更好的引流效果，标题是重中之重。但现在，封面图将会比标题更加重要。</span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">     </span><img class=\" aligncenter\" style=\"font-size: 11pt; width: 645px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important;\" title=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/2-1597587594.png\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？-20200817早读课\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" width=\"1545\" height=\"auto\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">③ 利用视频号账号引流</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">另外，通过使用“视频号账号”去热门视频下蹭流量也可以作为常规引流手段了。</span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\" aligncenter\" style=\"width: 645px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important;\" title=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/5-1597587595.png\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？-20200817早读课\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" width=\"842\" height=\"auto\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">④ 明确运营目的，关注变现闭环</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">最后也是最关键的一点，就是一定要明确运营目的，关注变现闭环。是要做广告、卖货，还是引流？然后，再去思考，要给用户提供什么内容。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">这个问题不搞清楚，就非常容易踩坑。</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">比如，运营研究社公众号的内容主要是运营干货、商业分析、行业内幕等方向，而且这些内容都很火。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">我们认为，它们值得用短视频再火一遍。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">因此，我们一开始做视频号的定位就是“分享奇葩的互联网运营套路”。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\" aligncenter\" style=\"font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Helvetica Neue', 'PingFang SC', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'Microsoft YaHei UI', 'Microsoft YaHei', Arial, sans-serif; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; white-space: normal; width: 645px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important;\" title=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/3-1597587595.png\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？-20200817早读课\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">发了几条视频之后，我们开始反思，要不要继续走这样的定位。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">在反思过程中，我们发现了一个问题。</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">最开始的时候，我们并没有把我们做短视频的目的想得非常细致，只是想要引流到我们的微信私域，然后做服务和变现。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">但按照我们当时的内容定位，就算把用户引流到我们的私域，我们提供的服务可能也跟用户想要的不匹配，用户可能也不会对我们的产品产生付费的需求。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">因此，我们做了一个非常具象的思考，<span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong>我们做视频号的目的是什么？</strong></span></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">最直接的目的是引流。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">引流的目的是什么呢？</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">我们希望用户购买我们的付费产品。</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">问完自己这 2 个问题，我们做视频号的目标就清晰了。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">我们希望<span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong>用户在我们的视频号中有收获，并且信任我们、认可我们，</strong></span>最终能够（在有需求的情况下）购买我们的课程和知识周边。</span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">   </span><img class=\" aligncenter\" style=\"font-size: 11pt; width: 645px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important;\" title=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/10-1597587597.png\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？-20200817早读课\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" width=\"undefined\" height=\"undefined\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">根据这一目的，我们开始调整内容规划。</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">我们的视频号定位从“分享奇葩的运营套路”变成“你的运营成长顾问”，从带运营人“猎奇”，变成帮助运营人成长。</span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">内容上，也从输出“奇葩的运营干货”转变为输出“实用的运营干货”，例如运营工作中需要的工具、简单的运营小技巧等等。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">在我们改变内容策略后，<span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong>发布的前两条视频就成为小爆款。</strong></span></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">而且，经常会有用户在视频下面咨询问题，或者提问怎么联系我们，这说明，用户认可我们的专业度，相信我们能帮他们解决一些运营问题。</span><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\" aligncenter\" style=\"width: 645px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important;\" title=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/6-1597587598.png\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？-20200817早读课\" alt=\"微信又来一波大改版，这次有多“香”？\" /></p>\n<h2 style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px; font-size: 18px;\">03</span></strong></span></h2>\n<h2 style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px; font-size: 18px;\">结语 </span></strong></span></h2>\n<section>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">下面，我们来总结下这次视频号改版，我们该如何应对：</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">① 做好私域流量的精细化运营；</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">② 改版后，封面图会比标题更重要；</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">③ 将视频号账号评论，作为常规引流手段；</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">④ 明确运营目的，关注变现闭环。</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">总的来看，这次改版对于视频号的运营者来说，绝对是真香。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">但我们也能看到改版背后的<span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong>一些问题：</strong></span></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span></p>\n<blockquote>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #888888;\">比如，不止一位朋友向我抱怨：因为点赞会将视频推荐给好友，所以他们现在一律不点赞。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #888888;\">再比如，视频内容、图文内容越来越多的功能在微信上“杀用户时间\"，这对于一个社交聊天 App 来说，是不是过于臃肿了？</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #888888;\">……</span></p>\n</blockquote>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\"> </span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; color: #3f3f3f; letter-spacing: 1px;\">微信会如何解决这些问题呢？我们拭目以待吧。</span></p>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n</section>\n<section>\n<div><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\">          来源：运营研究社（ID：U_quan）。作者授权早读课发表，转载请联系作者。</span></div>\n<div><span 650_f910dc314a4005f3.webp","https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/10-1597587593.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx27/cdn55@2020_2/2020/08/24/14-48-20-036_b2c399e94b4c2c1d.webp","https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/7-1597587593.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn20@2020_1/2020/08/24/14-48-00-173_11fc635a285c4a88.webp","https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/2-1597587594.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn96@2020_3/2020/08/24/14-48-57-289_754724a2b9f4315d.webp","https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/5-1597587595.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn7@2020_1/2020/08/24/14-48-48-627_d07c3ea6ea0cecad.webp","https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/3-1597587595.png":null,"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/10-1597587597.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx/cdn44@2020_3/2020/08/24/14-47-52-727_fc490baff3a108ab.webp","https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/6-1597587598.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn16@2020_2/2020/08/24/14-48-18-919_337b15c8fd57b8fe.webp","https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/09/8-1569159560.jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx31/cdn12@2020_1/2020/08/24/14-47-12-361_785891e2720b3897.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598280429012},{"createdTime":"2020-08-24 #3f3f3f;\">关晓彤的新剧《二十不惑》刚刚开播，第一集就戳中了不少观众的心。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">女主的室友姜小果，和同学闹了别扭，独自散步时，接到了妈妈的电话。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">妈妈带着歉意小心翼翼地询问小果：</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">“你说那个微信提现，我到现在也不会，你能不能再教教妈呀？”</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\">\n<section><img class=\"rich_pages aligncenter\" style=\"float: line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">姜小果翻了个白眼，瞬间狂躁：</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">“怎么又是这问题，我不是跟你说了嘛，你把微信钱包打开。”</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">妈妈语气更加讨好：“我这跟你打着电话呢，怎么打开微信呢？”</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">姜小果急到跳脚：</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">“我不之前都教过你了吗？”</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">“我都跟你说了那么多遍了，你还是不清楚！”</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">“我说一百遍，你还是不清楚啊！”</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages __bg_gif aligncenter\" style=\"width: 645px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important;\" title=\"为什么还有人在淘宝买老人机\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/3-1597511997.gif\" alt=\"为什么还有人在淘宝买老人机-2020-0816早读课\" alt=\"为什么还有人在淘宝买老人机\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">年轻人眼里好用又便利的智能手机，对许多老人来说，是一场“灾难”。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">这并不夸张。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">不会扫码，不懂转账，不知道网购怎么操作，最基础的聊天打电话也要翻来覆去研究许久……</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">淘宝搜索“老人机”，销量排名第一的那一款，有37万条评论，月销量是6.5万多台。</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">有人觉得难以置信：</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">“所有年轻人都在追求手机配置更高、功能更全的时候，还有这么多人在用这样的‘老古董’。”</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">我们似乎一边享受着“二维码时代”的便利，一边把那些不会使用智能手机的长辈们，远远抛在了身后。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages aligncenter\" style=\"text-align: center; box-shadow: #aaaaaa 0px 0px 14px 0px; width: 645px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important;\" title=\"为什么还有人在淘宝买老人机\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/5-1597511997.png\" alt=\"为什么还有人在淘宝买老人机-2020-0816早读课\" alt=\"为什么还有人在淘宝买老人机\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\">\n<h2 style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 18px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">01</span></strong></span></h2>\n<h2 style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 18px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">被迫走出“舒适区”的老人们</span></strong></span></h2>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\">\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">有人研究了一万多条电商平台评论，发现几乎一半人都提到了老人、长辈。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">父母公婆、爷爷奶奶、外公外婆、邻居老人……都是赠送对象。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">还有一些人，甚至多次购买同一款手机。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">满意理由也很简单：</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">字大、声音大、操作简单、价格实惠、待机时间长……</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">对老人而言，手机不需要太多花里胡哨的功能，能打电话发短信已经足够。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">可是，无处不在的二维码，越来越普遍网上预约、网上购票，都在强迫他们走出老人机的“舒适区”。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">一份征集老人与智能机故事的帖子里，有网友提起自己的卖菜的爷爷。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">爷爷因为没有智能机，无法使用手机收款，菜总是卖不出去：</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">“一点点菜，爷爷从早坐到晚，别人一来就问有没有收款码，他满是无助。”</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">也有人说起在医院遇到不会用手机挂号的老奶奶：</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">“老人家在收银台徘徊了好久，最后叹息一声走了……”</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages aligncenter\" style=\"text-align: center; width: 645px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important;\" title=\"为什么还有人在淘宝买老人机\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/8-1597511998.jpeg\" alt=\"为什么还有人在淘宝买老人机\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">今年上半年，一个健康码，给防疫工作带来无限便捷。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">可是，有些老人因为不会扫码，出行都成了难题。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">黑龙江，一位老人想出小区，被工作人员拦住，要求他出示健康码。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">老人解释自己用的老人机，无法扫码。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">工作人员坚持一定要出示二维码才能通行，争执中，老人被一把推开。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">手机摔在地上，老人去捡，重复了好几遍：<strong>“干啥啊？你干啥啊？”</strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages __bg_gif aligncenter\" style=\"text-align: center; width: 645px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important;\" title=\"为什么还有人在淘宝买老人机\" 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">到了门口被保安拦下，两方推搡起来，大爷被气到说不出话：</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span line-height: 1.75em;\">\n<h2 style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 18px;\">02</span></strong></span></h2>\n<h2 style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px; font-size: 18px;\">不是不想学，而是无处学</span></strong></span></h2>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\">\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">任何在我15-35岁之间诞生的科技，都将会是改变世界的革命性产物；</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">任何在我35岁以后诞生的科技，都是违反自然秩序的异端。”</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">我们眼中稀松平常的东西，已经是违反父母生活秩序的“异端”，怎能迅速坦然地接受？</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">看过一部短片：</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">一位已经退休的老父亲，去应聘一个实习生岗位，面试官问他为什么，他讲起自己的故事。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">和女儿一起吃饭，看到她桌子上的账单，父亲提出想帮女儿支付。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">女儿头也不抬：“不用，爸，它自己会付的。”</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">后来，父亲跑到营业厅去问，被人笑话不懂网络自动扣费。</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages __bg_gif aligncenter\" margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">可是，明明在“过时”之前，他也曾“无所不能”。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">去年春运期间，上海火车站有一位老人，为了买一张回安徽老家的火车票，跑了6躺火车站。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">所以很多时候，不是父母不愿意接受新事物，而是没有人愿意去教他们。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">电视剧里，姜小果因为教妈妈用微信暴跳如雷时，弹幕上几乎所有人都在感叹：</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">“太真实了，天下妈妈都一样，仿佛看到了我妈。”</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">“一模一样，我当时直接炸了……”</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">一面，是被时代“抛弃”的慌乱无助；</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">一面，是被儿女“嫌弃”的心酸孤独。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">他们似乎只能认命，只能看着自己越来越“渺小”，越来越过时……</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\">\n<h2 style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 18px;\">03</span></strong></span></h2>\n<h2 style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px; font-size: 18px;\">你是爸妈唯一的“解药”</span></strong></span></h2>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\">\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">不得不承认，很多时候，我们的孝顺，太过“一厢情愿”。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">朋友聊起自己给爸妈买了高档智能手机，过年回家才发现，两部手机都被小心收藏在柜子里。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">问爸妈为什么不用，他们只是笑笑：“我们老了，就不赶这个时髦了。”</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">后来他才得知，手机刚开始使用时，要设置新ID，爸妈一起研究了好几天都没弄明白怎么用，也没好意思问他，怕打扰他工作。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">后来又听说手机很贵，二老怕摆弄坏了，干脆收了起来。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">以为买了好手机给爸妈，就算尽了孝心。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">可这反而让爸妈觉得自己已经“年老无用”。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">我们眼中再简单不过的事情，对他们或许就难如登天；</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">他们的视力、听力、记忆力都在慢慢衰退，可我们很少意识到这种改变。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">一厢情愿地给予我们眼里的“好东西”，却一再忽略他们的真实需求，这不是孝顺，这是自私。</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">很多人，内心把父母放在最重要的位置上，但日常行动中，父母又总是排在后面：</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">领导同事工作群的微信，必须秒回，爸妈的消息，想起来了就回，忙了干脆忽略。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">对难缠的客户报以最大的耐心和宽容，对父母偶尔的打扰满心不耐烦。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">看到网上有人为父母详细绘制智能手机使用教程，感动地点赞转发收藏；</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">可轮到自己，匆匆教上一两遍，就耐心告罄……</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">实在不公平。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\" aligncenter\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; width: 640px !important; visibility: visible !important;\" title=\"为什么还有人在淘宝买老人机\" src=\"https://www.zaodula.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/2-1597512005.jpeg\" alt=\"为什么还有人在淘宝买老人机\" width=\"640\" height=\"751\" /></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">对很多老人来说，儿女是他们唯一一扇看世界的窗。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">科技带给我们惊喜，却带给他们慌乱。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">我们的耐心和爱，是唯一治愈慌乱的“解药”。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">你必须让父母知道，他们可以询问你、麻烦你，无论多少遍，你永远对他们有耐心。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">这样，他们才不会在某一天变成那位火车站里下跪求票的爷爷、变成小区门口被人推搡的大爷……</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">我们都不是聪明伶俐的学生，小时候，学用筷子要花几个周，学走路、学说话更是要耗费爸妈无数时间精力。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">那时，他们毫无怨言。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px;\">如今，轮到我们带领、陪伴、保护他们，去面对这个飞速变化的世界。</span></strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">不妨学一学，他们当初的耐心。</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">“孝顺这个词，是由后悔组成的。”</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">父母已经在变老了，他们白发越来越多，身体越来越弱，对医院越来越熟悉……</span></p>\n<p style=\"margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 8px; line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; color: #3f3f3f;\">今生能够相伴的日子，每一天都在减少。</span></p>\n</div>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<div class=\"single-content\">\n<div class=\"bpp-post-content\">\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<section></section>\n<section
